 </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:14pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center"><B>Important Notice Regarding the Availability of Proxy Materials for the </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:14pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center"><B>Exxon Mobil Corporation Shareholder Meeting to be Held on May 30, 2018 </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:14pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:ARIAL">Under Securities and Exchange Commission rules, you are receiving this Notice that the proxy materials for the annual shareholders&#146; meeting are available on the
Internet. Follow the instructions below to view the materials and vote online or request a copy. The items to be voted on and location of the annual meeting are on the reverse side. Your vote is important! </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:14pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>This communication presents only an overview of the more complete proxy materials that are available to you on the Internet. We encourage you to access and review

STYLE="font-size:5pt" COLOR="#ff001a">&nbsp;</FONT>Why am I receiving this Notice of Internet Availability? &nbsp;&nbsp;</B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:3pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:1pt">&nbsp;</P></TD></TR>
</TABLE></DIV> <DIV ALIGN="right">
<TABLE CELLSPACING="0" CELLPADDING="0" WIDTH="92%" BORDER="0" STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt">


<TR>
<TD WIDTH="100%"></TD></TR>


<TR STYLE="page-break-inside:avoid ; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt">
<TD VALIGN="top">Pursuant to the SEC &#147;Notice and Access&#148; proxy rules, companies are permitted to send the enclosed &#147;Notice&#148; instead of a full printed set of proxy materials. The Notice gives you instructions on how to view your
company&#146;s proxy materials and vote online, or how to receive a full set of printed materials by mail.</TD></TR>
<TR STYLE="font-size:1pt">
<TD HEIGHT="10"></TD></TR>
<TR STYLE="page-break-inside:avoid ; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt">
<TD VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL">There are several advantages to your company sending a Notice instead of a full set of materials including lowering your company&#146;s costs, and
reducing the environmental impact from printing and mailing full sets of proxy materials.</P> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:1pt">&nbsp;</P></TD></TR></TABLE></DIV>
<DIV ALIGN="right">
<TABLE CELLSPACING="0" CELLPADDING="0" WIDTH="93%" BORDER="0" STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:9pt">
